use music_world_db;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS singers;
CREATE TABLE singers (
  singer_id int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  image varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  nationality varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` text,
  birth_year smallint DEFAULT NULL,
  gender tinyint NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (singer_id)
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS albums;
CREATE TABLE albums (
  album_id int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  released_date date DEFAULT NULL,
  singer_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  image varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  views int DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (album_id),
  KEY albums_singers_fk (singer_id),
  CONSTRAINT albums_singers_fk FOREIGN KEY (singer_id) REFERENCES singers (singer_id)
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS articles;
CREATE TABLE articles (
  article_id int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  title mediumtext NOT NULL,
  thumbnail varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` mediumtext,
  `url` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  singer_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (article_id),
  KEY singer_id_fk (singer_id),
  CONSTRAINT singer_id_fk FOREIGN KEY (singer_id) REFERENCES singers (singer_id)
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS categories;
CREATE TABLE categories (
  category_id int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (category_id)
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS songs;
CREATE TABLE songs (
  song_id int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  released_date date DEFAULT NULL,
  lyrics text,
  file_name varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  image varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  views int DEFAULT NULL,
  category_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  album_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (song_id),
  KEY songs_categories_fk (category_id),
  KEY songs_albums_fk (album_id),
  CONSTRAINT songs_albums_fk FOREIGN KEY (album_id) REFERENCES albums (album_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT songs_categories_fk FOREIGN KEY (category_id) REFERENCES categories (category_id) ON DELETE SET NULL
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS songs_singers;
CREATE TABLE songs_singers (
  song_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  singer_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  KEY songs_singers_songs_fk (song_id),
  KEY songs_singers_singers_fk (singer_id),
  CONSTRAINT songs_singers_singers_fk FOREIGN KEY (singer_id) REFERENCES singers (singer_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT songs_singers_songs_fk FOREIGN KEY (song_id) REFERENCES songs (song_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS users;
CREATE TABLE users (
  user_id int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  username varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `password` text NOT NULL,
  email varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `role` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  review_id int DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id),
  UNIQUE KEY users_pk (username),
  UNIQUE KEY users_pk3 (email)
);
